<rating>5<//rating>< review>
Had towing hitch + wiring installed on my '17 Mercedes E300 Sedan a couple weeks back. Newer model Mercedes vehicles are definitely not easy to work on and I specifically did not want any wire splicing to prevent OEM warranty loss. After researching google reviews and yelp, Uhaul of Thornton seemed to have most positive ratings for hitch install, despite they are far from where I live. In the end, the longer drive was more than worth it.

Outstanding installation service - performed very cleanly and at extremely reasonable pricing. Tried the Zero Contact Module for wiring, which did not work. But was recommended a pinch type wiring (Similar to posi-tap/ No splicing) which worked perfectly. Have utilized the hitch to carry bike racks and to tow UHaul motorcycle trailers. Hitch and wiring have functioned 100% perfectly. Highly recommended for hitch installs. Overall service experience was remarkable. Will return for any and all of my future hitch install needs. Thank you Uhaul of Thornton - keep up this good work.< /review>

< Review>
To start off, I wasn't informed of the option to have 24hr access to my storage unit, and they rented me a unit on the interior of one of the buildings which I thus didn't know was inaccessible after store hours. I arrived at 7:10pm with a pickup-load of stuff to find the staff closing up the store, and all the buildings were locked with no way to get into my unit. I had to haul everything back home and unload it back into my garage.

In trying to rent and deal with delivery of a U-Box later to move my stuff out of the storage unit and cross-country, I seldom was able to speak to a rep at the store; nearly every call rolled over to the national call center, whose staff couldn't really handle things that were store-specific, and my calls were only returned by store staff about 10% of the time. Generally, I always had to call and leave messages multiple times to get a call back for anything, and the cumulative result was that my cross-country move was delayed more than 10 days, and they missed getting my U-Box delivered by the end of the month, thus forcing me to pay for an extra month of rent on the storage unit.

The original quote that I received for the U-Box was somehow misplaced and not logged electronically such that the national U-Box customer service people could see it when I called to confirm my reservation a couple days before it was supposed to be available, and they told me the price would be $400 more than the original quote. Only after leaving messages for the store over the course of 4 days, and finally being escalated to the regional manager's voicemail and waiting a few more days for a call back, was I able to get them to dig up and honor the original price.

Worse, my U-Box was not forklifted into position on time, even though I'd called the day before to make sure they had plenty of notice to have things ready. I had to call the store to find out what was wrong, my call rolled over (again) to the national call center, I explained my predicament and was transferred to a regional manager, and she messaged and called the manager at the Thornton location directly to finally get someone to move the U-Box. My movers, who were being paid by the hour, waited for 25 minutes on the clock (my dime) before they could start working.

If things had gone less-than-swimmingly a few times, that's everyday life, and I would understand. As it was, I was held hostage to a pattern of inattention and failure to follow through over a period of multiple weeks that cost me a bunch of extra money, delayed my move, and was a real pain to try to resolve.

As I write this, I've been waiting all afternoon for a call back to set up shipment of my U-Box.<//Review>

<Rating>5< /Rating>< text>
I was referred to Dr. Liang because my cataracts were greatly limiting my everyday life - keeping me from driving at night or on trips to unfamiliar places. At age 69, I wanted to have optimum sight now, while I could still be physically active.

Dr. Liang's office staff were all exceptionally kind and skilled at what they do.The intake process taught me so many things about the state of my vision and what could be done to improve it.

I had the first eye surgery one week ago. The procedure was quick and not painful. I had one day of slight discomfort and within two more days, I was driving my car without wearing glasses! The impact of that improved vision is amazing! I now feel at ease and confident in my driving, and also feel much more solid on the ground when walking or hiking.

I just scheduled surgery for the second eye and can't wait. It's likely both eyes will return to 2020 distance vision.

There are several options for improving your vision, and Dr. Liang's office will lead you through each of those choices. If you're contemplating cataract surgery, I highly recommend you have an evaluation by Dr. Keith Liang.</text>

I am a very active person and love playing sports, snowboarding, swimming, etc. When I was dependent upon contacts, it was a hassle and huge inconvenience to do those things without worrying about my contacts drying up or falling out. An "oldie but a goodie" on Santana Row. In the before times it was a great venue for birthday parties and private events, now it's a great spot for outdoor dining. The patio on the side has heat lamps overhead to keep diners comfortable. The tables on the street has freestanding heat lamps.

< Review>
Pros:
- Food was great, decent portions for the price
- ambiance is awesome, feels like sitting right on Santana Row.

Cons:
- terribly understaffed
- orders weren't just right. We asked for no straws in our drinks, and we got straws. We asked for extra spicy entrees and they were mild.

We went on July 3, and they had two main hostesses that were taking orders on our half of the restaurant. It took forever for us to get our checks and that really soured our mood, but those hostesses were doing all they could. The orders being off is probably a result of how understaffed they were.

The dishes were great though, and the drinks were interesting. Also, 6 people ate, along with drinks for $200 before tip (we shared dishes), which I think is a good price, especially considering it's on Santana Row.< /Review>

< review>
Great location right along Santana Row

If you arrive just before dinner time, you can easily get seated. The hostesses were very accommodating with my need to work and eat and plug in my laptop. They seated me in an area where I could do my phone calls and work while I ate. The menu is different if you are seated at the lounge vs the dining area and drinks are different prices too.

Menu selection is great in both the dining area and lounge. Lots of exotic dishes that is a fusion of American and Asian cuisine. Prices aren‚Äôt too bad with a lot of entr√©e dishes under $30. Beverage selection is pretty good and prices are average. The portions are a little on the small side but very tasty. Service was good from the time you are seated to the time you finish off. They didn‚Äôt have any issues with me moving about the restaurant and changing tables.

It gets a little loud as the night progresses because of the music and a different crowd encroaches. It seems like a usual hangout for business visitors though.

I ordered the Pan Seared Salmon for $20. It was really unique with all my favourite flavours mixed in from cilantro to lemongrass chili sambal and mango salsa sauce. Salmon was done perfectly. I would go back again but the only unfortunate thing about Santana Row is that most of the restaurants are closed by around 11pm.</review>
